
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Define variables for each cell in the 2x3 grid and express the given sum conditions as algebraic equations.'}, {'objective': 'Derive constraints on the digits from the equations representing the sums of the two numbers formed by rows and the three numbers formed by columns.'}, {'objective': 'Enumerate all possible digit assignments in the 2x3 grid that satisfy the derived constraints.'}, {'objective': 'Count the total number of valid digit placements that meet both the row and column sum conditions.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The problem involves a 2x3 grid, i.e., 2 rows and 3 columns, with each cell containing a single digit (0-9).
- Two numbers are formed by reading the rows left to right: the first row forms a 3-digit number, and the second row forms another 3-digit number.
- The sum of these two 3-digit numbers is 999.
- Three numbers are formed by reading the columns top to bottom: each column forms a 2-digit number (top digit as tens place, bottom digit as units place).
- The sum of these three 2-digit numbers is 99.
- An example grid is provided:
  \[
  \begin{array}{|c|c|c|} \hline
  0 & 0 & 8 \\ \hline
  9 & 9 & 1 \\ \hline
  \end{array}
  \]
  where the row sums are 8 + 991 = 999 and the column sums are 9 + 9 + 81 = 99.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The digits in the grid are variables constrained by the sum conditions.
- The row sums condition: (100a + 10b + c) + (100d + 10e + f) = 999, where a,b,c,d,e,f are digits in the grid.
- The column sums condition: (10a + d) + (10b + e) + (10c + f) = 99.
- The constraints imply dependencies between digits across rows and columns.
- The problem requires counting the number of digit assignments satisfying both sum conditions simultaneously.
- The example shows that digits can be zero, and leading zeros are allowed in the numbers formed by rows and columns.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in combinatorics and number theory.
- It involves discrete mathematics, specifically counting digit assignments under arithmetic constraints.
- Concepts include place value, digit sums, and combinatorial enumeration.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and recreational mathematics.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- It is not explicitly stated whether leading zeros are allowed in the numbers formed by rows or columns, though the example suggests they are.
- The problem does not specify if digits can be repeated or if any digit restrictions apply beyond being a single digit.
- Potential challenges include handling multiple constraints simultaneously and ensuring all digit assignments are valid.
- The problem may have multiple solutions or configurations, requiring careful enumeration.
============== task decomposition 0 ================
{'stage_0': {'subtask_1': {'objective': 'Derive formal algebraic expressions representing the sum constraints for the rows and columns of the 2x3 digit grid, and validate these expressions against the example provided.', 'dependencies': [], 'agent_collaboration': 'SC_CoT'}}, 'stage_1': {'subtask_1': {'objective': 'Enumerate and verify all possible digit assignments for the grid cells that satisfy the row sum constraint (sum of two 3-digit numbers equals 999).', 'dependencies': ['stage_0.subtask_1'], 'agent_collaboration': 'Debate'}, 'subtask_2': {'objective': 'Enumerate and verify all possible digit assignments for the grid cells that satisfy the column sum constraint (sum of three 2-digit numbers equals 99).', 'dependencies': ['stage_0.subtask_1'], 'agent_collaboration': 'Debate'}}, 'stage_2': {'subtask_1': {'objective': 'Decompose the combined constraints from the row and column sums to identify digit value dependencies and simplify the search space for valid digit assignments.', 'dependencies': ['stage_1.subtask_1', 'stage_1.subtask_2'], 'agent_collaboration': 'Reflexion'}}, 'stage_3': {'subtask_1': {'objective': 'Aggregate and combine the simplified digit assignments to count the total number of valid 2x3 digit grids satisfying both sum constraints simultaneously.', 'dependencies': ['stage_0.subtask_1', 'stage_2.subtask_1'], 'agent_collaboration': 'SC_CoT'}}}
============== code generate 0 ================
async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_sc_instruction_0 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Derive formal algebraic expressions representing the sum constraints for the rows and columns of the 2x3 digit grid, "
        "and validate these expressions against the example provided. The grid cells are variables a,b,c,d,e,f representing digits. "
        "Row sum: (100a + 10b + c) + (100d + 10e + f) = 999. Column sum: (10a + d) + (10b + e) + (10c + f) = 99. "
        "Confirm these expressions and their correctness with the example grid provided."
    )
    N_sc = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_0 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_sc)]
    possible_answers_0 = []
    possible_thinkings_0 = []
    subtask_desc_0 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_0.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_0,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N_sc):
        thinking0, answer0 = await cot_agents_0[i]([taskInfo], cot_sc_instruction_0, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_0[i].id}, deriving algebraic expressions, thinking: {thinking0.content}; answer: {answer0.content}")
        possible_answers_0.append(answer0)
        possible_thinkings_0.append(thinking0)
    final_decision_agent_0 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking0, answer0 = await final_decision_agent_0([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_0 + possible_answers_0, 
        "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and choose the most consistent and correct algebraic expressions for the sum constraints.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking0.content}; answer - {answer0.content}")
    subtask_desc_0['response'] = {"thinking": thinking0, "answer": answer0}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_0)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    debate_instruction_row = (
        "Sub-task 1: Enumerate and verify all possible digit assignments for the grid cells that satisfy the row sum constraint: "
        "(100a + 10b + c) + (100d + 10e + f) = 999, where a,b,c,d,e,f are digits 0-9. "
        "Given the algebraic expressions from stage 0, find all valid assignments for the row sums. "
        "Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    )
    debate_instruction_col = (
        "Sub-task 2: Enumerate and verify all possible digit assignments for the grid cells that satisfy the column sum constraint: "
        "(10a + d) + (10b + e) + (10c + f) = 99, where a,b,c,d,e,f are digits 0-9. "
        "Given the algebraic expressions from stage 0, find all valid assignments for the column sums. "
        "Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    )

    debate_agents_row = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]
    debate_agents_col = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]
    N_max_debate = self.max_round

    all_thinking_row = [[] for _ in range(N_max_debate)]
    all_answer_row = [[] for _ in range(N_max_debate)]
    all_thinking_col = [[] for _ in range(N_max_debate)]
    all_answer_col = [[] for _ in range(N_max_debate)]

    subtask_desc_row = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_1.subtask_1",
        "instruction": debate_instruction_row,
        "context": ["user query", thinking0.content, answer0.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    subtask_desc_col = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_1.subtask_2",
        "instruction": debate_instruction_col,
        "context": ["user query", thinking0.content, answer0.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }

    for r in range(N_max_debate):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_row):
            if r == 0:
                thinking_r, answer_r = await agent([taskInfo, thinking0, answer0], debate_instruction_row, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_r = [taskInfo, thinking0, answer0] + all_thinking_row[r-1] + all_answer_row[r-1]
                thinking_r, answer_r = await agent(input_infos_r, debate_instruction_row, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, row sum constraint, thinking: {thinking_r.content}; answer: {answer_r.content}")
            all_thinking_row[r].append(thinking_r)
            all_answer_row[r].append(answer_r)

        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_col):
            if r == 0:
                thinking_c, answer_c = await agent([taskInfo, thinking0, answer0], debate_instruction_col, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_c = [taskInfo, thinking0, answer0] + all_thinking_col[r-1] + all_answer_col[r-1]
                thinking_c, answer_c = await agent(input_infos_c, debate_instruction_col, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, column sum constraint, thinking: {thinking_c.content}; answer: {answer_c.content}")
            all_thinking_col[r].append(thinking_c)
            all_answer_col[r].append(answer_c)

    final_decision_agent_row = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_row, answer_row = await final_decision_agent_row([taskInfo, thinking0, answer0] + all_thinking_row[-1] + all_answer_row[-1], 
        "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and choose the most consistent digit assignments satisfying the row sum constraint.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output (row sums): thinking - {thinking_row.content}; answer - {answer_row.content}")
    subtask_desc_row['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_row, "answer": answer_row}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_row)
    print("Step 2 (row sums): ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_decision_agent_col = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_col, answer_col = await final_decision_agent_col([taskInfo, thinking0, answer0] + all_thinking_col[-1] + all_answer_col[-1], 
        "Sub-task 2: Synthesize and choose the most consistent digit assignments satisfying the column sum constraint.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output (column sums): thinking - {thinking_col.content}; answer - {answer_col.content}")
    subtask_desc_col['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_col, "answer": answer_col}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_col)
    print("Step 2 (column sums): ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction = (
        "Sub-task 1: Decompose the combined constraints from the row and column sums to identify digit value dependencies and simplify the search space for valid digit assignments. "
        + reflect_inst
    )
    cot_agent_reflect = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_reflect = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_reflect = [taskInfo, thinking_row, answer_row, thinking_col, answer_col]
    subtask_desc_reflect = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_2.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_row.content, answer_row.content, thinking_col.content, answer_col.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking_reflect, answer_reflect = await cot_agent_reflect(cot_inputs_reflect, cot_reflect_instruction, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_reflect.id}, decomposing combined constraints, thinking: {thinking_reflect.content}; answer: {answer_reflect.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_reflect):
        critic_inst = "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'"
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent([taskInfo, thinking_reflect, answer_reflect], critic_inst, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_reflect.extend([thinking_reflect, answer_reflect, feedback])
        thinking_reflect, answer_reflect = await cot_agent_reflect(cot_inputs_reflect, cot_reflect_instruction, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_reflect.id}, refining decomposition, thinking: {thinking_reflect.content}; answer: {answer_reflect.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking_reflect.content}; answer - {answer_reflect.content}")
    subtask_desc_reflect['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_reflect, "answer": answer_reflect}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_reflect)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_3 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Aggregate and combine the simplified digit assignments to count the total number of valid 2x3 digit grids satisfying both sum constraints simultaneously. "
        "Use the decomposed constraints and simplifications from previous stages to enumerate and count all valid assignments."
    )
    cot_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_sc)]
    possible_answers_3 = []
    possible_thinkings_3 = []
    subtask_desc_3 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_3.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking0.content, answer0.content, thinking_reflect.content, answer_reflect.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N_sc):
        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agents_3[i]([taskInfo, thinking0, answer0, thinking_reflect, answer_reflect], cot_sc_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_3[i].id}, aggregating and counting valid assignments, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
        possible_answers_3.append(answer3)
        possible_thinkings_3.append(thinking3)
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo, thinking0, answer0, thinking_reflect, answer_reflect] + possible_thinkings_3 + possible_answers_3, 
        "Sub-task 5: Synthesize and provide the total count of valid 2x3 digit grids satisfying both sum constraints.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc_3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking3, "answer": answer3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_3)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking3, answer3, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

The digits in the top row are (a,b,c), and in the bottom row are (d,e,f), with each digit in [0,9]. The sum of the two numbers formed by the rows is 999, which implies the digit-level complement relation: d = 9 - a, e = 9 - b, f = 9 - c. The sum of the three two-digit numbers formed by the columns is 99, i.e., (10a + d) + (10b + e) + (10c + f) = 99. Substituting the complement relation, this sum becomes 10(a + b + c) + (d + e + f) = 10(a + b + c) + 27 - (a + b + c) = 9(a + b + c) + 27 = 99. Solving for a + b + c gives a + b + c = 8. Define S = a + b + c and T = d + e + f. Since d + e + f = 27 - S, we have T = 27 - S. The column sum can be expressed as 10S + T = 99.
